<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon Posts 12.5 Percent Rise in Second Quarter Sales</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Second Quarter Highlights</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland &#8211; July 26, 2010 &#8211; </font>Alcon, Inc. (NYSE:ACL) reported that global sales rose 12.5 percent to $1.89 billion for the second quarter of 2010, or 11.3 percent excluding the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations and acquisitions.&#160;&#160;Revenue from acquisitions added 40 basis points to sales growth in the quarter, while foreign currency fluctuations added 80 basis points of growth.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Net earnings for the second quarter of 2010 grew 15.1 percent to $670 million, or $2.21 per diluted share, compared to $582 million, or $1.94 per diluted share in the second quarter of 2009.&#160;&#160;Non-GAAP adjusted net earnings would have grown 15.8 percent to $674 million, or $2.22 per diluted share, compared to second quarter 2009 net earnings.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Adjusted net earnings in the second quarter of 2010 exclude $4 million in other operating expenses related to the potential change of control and merger proposal from Novartis AG.&#160;&#160;Reconciliations of reported and adjusted results for the second quarter are included in the financial tables below.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;Our strong performance in the first half of this year was driven by the successful global execution of our operational strategies and was further supported by a lower first half comparison period.&#160;&#160;We have risen above the global reimbursement challenges in 2010 to achieve very positive organic sales growth at the Alcon group level and market share expansion of our key promoted brands on a global basis.&#160;&#160;Key growth drivers like advanced technology intraocular lenses, glaucoma treatments and emerging markets are providing both near-term and durable long-term opportunities,&#8221; said Kevin Buehler, Alcon&#8217;s president and chief executive officer.&#160;&#160;&#8220;These results and our outlook for the balance of the year reflect an improved market environment that we expect to support sustainable organic sal
es growth and operating leverage in the future.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Sales Highlights</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Summarized below are sales highlights for the second quarter of 2010. All growth comparisons are for the second quarter of 2010 compared to the second quarter of 2009. Organic sales growth rates exclude currency impacts and acquisitions and are non-GAAP measures that are reconciled in a table at the end of this release.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">U.S. sales increased 12.7 percent due to strong contributions from advanced technology <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AcrySof</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> intraocular lenses, healthy growth in glaucoma sales and the stronger seasonal impact of a severe allergy season on sales of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Patanol</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#174;</font> and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Pataday</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#174;</font> ophthalmic solutions and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Patanase<
/font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#174;</font> nasal spray.&#160;&#160;Sales growth included 90 basis points from acquisitions and also benefitted from a more favorable market environment when compared to the second quarter of 2009.</font></div>

</tr></table>

</tr></table>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Global glaucoma sales rose 17.2 percent organically (+17.5 percent reported). The <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Azopt</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> family of products (<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Azopt</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AZARGA</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> ophthalmic suspensions) increased 15.1 percent organically (+14.8 percent reported), led by continued market penetration of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AZARGA</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICA
L-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>outside the United States.&#160;&#160;Global sales of the <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TRAVATAN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>family of products (<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TRAVATAN</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font>,<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> TRAVATAN Z</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DuoTrav</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> ophthalmic solutions) rose 13.8 percent on an organic basis (+14.3 percent reported).</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Global sales of allergy products rose 31.9 percent on an organic basis (+32.5 percent reported) as the severe allergy season in the United States drove sales of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Patanol</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#174;</font> and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Pataday</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#174;</font> ophthalmic solutions.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Financial Guidance</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The company raised its full year 2010 guidance for organic sales growth from the mid-to-high single digits to the high single digits.&#160;&#160;It also raised its earnings per share guidance to a range of $7.45 to $7.62.&#160;&#160;The higher guidance includes the impact of European fiscal austerity actions, a currency headwind in the second half of the year and higher research and development spending on internal projects as well as business development initiatives.&#160;&#160;The guidance includes the on-going impact of health care reform, which is expected to reduce full year 2010 sales by $20 million and earnings per share by $0.06.&#160;&#160;Full year guidance excludes costs related to a potential change of control to and/or merger with Novartis and the first quarter impacts of a change in royalty estimate.&#160;&#160;It also exclu
des the catch-up impact of the change in tax treatment of U.S. retiree medical expenses related to U.S. health care reform. The full year guidance assumes renewal of the U.S. Research and Experimentation tax credit in the fourth quarter of 2010 with retroactive application.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company Description</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon, Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.5 billion in 2009.&#160; Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic industry for 65 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contacts lens solutions and other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions of the eye.&#160; Alcon operates in 75 countries and sells products in 180 markets.&#160; For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s web site at www.alcon.com.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">N/M - Not Meaningful</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Change in constant currency calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations. Management believes constant currency sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">N/M - Not Meaningful</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Change in constant currency calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations. Management believes constant currency sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div>
